For example:a)\u00a0 A basic office fitout can start at $600 Per Square Metre whereas a premium office fitout could cost you over $2000 Per Square Metreb)\u00a0 A basic retail fitout can start at $1000 Per Square Metre whereas a premium office fitout could cost you over $2000 Per Square Metrec) A basic restaurant fitout can start at $1800 Per Square Metre whereas a premium office fitout could cost you over $3400 Per Square MetreThese figures are intended as a guide only. commencing their shop fitout project.Typically, you require council approvals for all construction and shop fitout projects where you \u201cchange use\u201d of the existing building.An example of a \u201cchange of use\u201d would be if you change a tenancy which is currently used as an office building into a premises for shop use.\u00a0However, the exact council you require can vary depending on the council, the extent of the works and other factors.Top shop fit out companies will organise and liaise with a Private Certifying Authority or council on behalf of their client to simplify the process.Don\u2019t be afraid to ask a shop fit out company for copies of their insurance policies.Shop fitout companies are required to have public liability insurance, all risk insurance as well as workers compensation.If your builder is hesitant to share these documents with you, take this as a major red flag.To eliminate any of your concerns, it\u2019s a good idea to cross check with the insurance companies to determine if their policy is still valid or if they\u2019ve expired.It\u2019s better to be safe than sorry!This really depends on the project specifics and scope of work.In some 				<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">What is a fit out?</h3>
				<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p><span>Quite simply, a <a href="https://impeccabuild.com.au/commercial-fit-out/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">fit out</a> is a construction term that describes the process of making interior spaces suitable for occupation. </span></p>
<p><span><a href="https://impeccabuild.com.au/commercial-fit-out/">Commercial fit out</a> projects are often related to office developments, retail shops, restaurants, cafes and other commercial premises</span>.</p>
<p>It involves renovating the internal layout and interior space to meet the tenant’s requirements.</p>
<p><span>Very often, the base construction is completed by the developer and the final <a href="https://impeccabuild.com.au/commercial-fit-out/">commercial fit out</a> is done by the tenant</span>.<span> </span></p>
<p><span>A <a href="https://impeccabuild.com.au/commercial-fit-out/">commercial fit out</a> covers all activities relating to interior work including but not limited to: plumbing, carpentry, electrical, joinery, painting, flooring, and more..</span>.</p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_1  et_pb_toggle_close">
				
				
				
				
				<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">How much will my fitout project cost?</h3>
				<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
<div class="wpb_wrapper">
<p><span>When your business is considering an interior <a href="https://impeccabuild.com.au/retail-fit-out-costs/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">fit-out, some idea of ballpark costs</a> is always helpful but no two shop fit outs are ever the same, there are numerous variations that come into play, which makes it difficult to answer questions like how much does a fit out cost? </span></p>
<p><span>Costs vary project to project, by size, scope and industry. For example:</span></p>
<ul>
<li><span>A basic office fitout can start at $600 Per Square Metre whereas a premium office fitout could cost you over $2000 Per Square Metre</span></li>
<li><span>A basic retail fitout can start at $1000 Per Square Metre whereas a premium office fitout could cost you over $2000 Per Square Metre</span></li>
<li><span>A basic restaurant fitout can start at $1800 Per Square Metre whereas a premium office fitout could cost you over $3400 Per Square Metre</span></li>
</ul>
<p><span>These figures are intended as a guide only. We don’t operate a cookie-cutter approach to our work, providing we treat each client as a unique proposition. </span></p>
<p><span>It’s perfectly possible to mix and match features to create a custom solution that’s exactly right for what you’ve got in mind.</span></p>
<p><strong>Related information:</strong></p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="nectar-fancy-ul animated-in" data-list-icon="dot" data-animation="true" data-animation-delay="0" data-spacing="default" data-alignment="left">
<ul>
<li><a href="https://impeccabuild.com.au/fit-out/4-proven-tips-to-save-money-on-your-fit-out/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Want To Know How You Could Save Thousands On Your Fit-Out?</a></li>
<li><a href="https://impeccabuild.com.au/retail-fit-out-costs/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">How Much Will My Retail Store Build Cost?</a></li>

</ul>
</div></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_2  et_pb_toggle_close">
				
				
				
				
				<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">What Is A Shop Fit Out Contractor?</h3>
				<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p>We combine stunning aesthetic appeal with the need to create environments that work!</p>

			</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_3  et_pb_toggle_close">
				
				
				
				
				<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">How Long Will My Shop Fitout Project Take?</h3>
				<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p><span>Generally, a 200 square metre shop fitout project can be completed within 5-6 weeks. </span></p>
<p><span>However, the exact duration of a shop fit-out project can vary greatly depending on the requirements, the location, the size,  the materials/finishes selected, council approvals, and many other variables of your shop fitout project. </span></p>
<p><span>We understand that time is money therefore we provide our clients with a project timeline and schedule at the very start!</span></p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_4  et_pb_toggle_close">
				
				
				
				
				<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">Should I Choose The Cheapest Quote For My Shop Fit Out Project?</h3>
				<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p><span>Be very wary of falling into the trap of choosing the shop fitout company who provides the cheapest quote.</span></p>
<p><span>Firstly, Before deciding which shop fitout company you choose to award your project to, it is crucial to go through each quote you received thoroughly.</span></p>
<p><span>Cross-check each quote with your shop design plans to ensure nothing was left out. The more detailed the shop fitout quote the better!</span></p>
<p><span>One reason why a shop fitout quote may be significantly cheaper than another may be because a builder has left an item out, this could lead to variation claims in the future and you might actually end up spending more.</span></p></div>
			</div>
			</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_3 et_pb_column_44  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_blurb et_pb_blurb_18  et_pb_text_align_left  et_pb_blurb_position_top et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_blurb_content">
					<div class="et_pb_main_blurb_image"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap"><span class="et-waypoint et_pb_animation_off et_pb_animation_off_tablet et_pb_animation_off_phone et-pb-icon">&#x77;</span></span></div>
					<div class="et_pb_blurb_container">
						
						
					</div>
				</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_accordion et_pb_accordion_1">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_5  et_pb_toggle_open">
				
				
				
				
				<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">What is a fit out contractor?</h3>
				<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p>A fit out is completed by a fit out contractor, who<span> </span><a href="https://impeccabuild.com.au/design-services/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">designs</a><span> </span>and constructs any building work or building improvements that are required during the fit out process.</p>
<p>They will usually provide the material, labour and equipment that is required for the project and they will liaise with the client to ensure that they achieve the desired result.</p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_6  et_pb_toggle_close">
				
				
				
				
				<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">What Is A Shop Fit Out?</h3>
				<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p><span>Put simply, a shop fit out is a construction term that describes the process of making the interior of a space suitable for occupation for a shop business. </span></p>
<p><span>A shop fitout project involves renovating the internal layout and interior space to meet the tenant’s requirements. </span></p>
<p><span>Very often, the base construction is completed by the developer and the final shop fit out is the responsibility of the tenant. </span></p>
<p><span>A shop fit out project covers all activities relating to the interior construction and remodelling work including but not limited to: plumbing, carpentry, electrical, joinery, painting, flooring, and more…</span></p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_7  et_pb_toggle_close">
				
				
				
				
				<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">How Should I Choose A Shop Fit Out Company?</h3>
				<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p>Every member of our team is a time-served craftsman, committed to doing the very best job possible.</p>
<p>Any contractors we use are, like us, highly experienced tradesmen with a reputation for excellence.</p>
<p><span>With years of experience in the trade and strong local links, we are proud to have completed design projects for a wide range of Sydney businesses.</span></p>
<p><span>This diversity of work, combined with our commitment to staying ahead when it comes to design, means we have the expertise to successfully develop almost any commercial interior.</span></p>
<p><span>Familiar with relevant legislation and regulations, use us for: offices; retail; restaurants; franchises; gyms; clubs; clinics; surgeries; and more</span></p>
<ul>
<li>Enhanced efficiency.</li>
<li>Greater productivity.</li>
<li>Higher customer footfall.</li>
<li>Higher value sales.</li>
<li>Optimal working conditions for staff.</li>
<li>Appealing customer experience.</li>
<li>Low running and maintenance costs.</li>
<li>Inclusive environment that embraces diversity.</li>
</ul>
<p>Our fitouts are highly functional and designed to represent a sound economic investment that results in increased profits for your business.</p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_8  et_pb_toggle_close">
				
				
				
				
				<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">What Is The Process Of A Shop Fit Out Project ?</h3>
				<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p><span>It all starts with your initial consultation where we ask you some simple questions to try and understand what your requirements are and what is the most effective way for us to assist you in achieving your goals.</span></p>
<p><span>A typical shop fitout project from start to finish would be as follows:</span></p>
<p><span>1) Initial Consultation </span></p>
<p><span>2) Design Brief &amp; Shop Space Planning</span></p>
<p><span>3) Shop Concept Designs</span></p>
<p><span>4) Shop Fitout Costing Analysis</span></p>
<p><span>5) Compliance &amp; Regulation Checks </span></p>
<p><span>6) Shop Fitout Project Management</span></p>
<p><span>7) Hand-Over Of Completed Shop Space</span></p>
<p><span>8) Ongoing After-Project Support</span></p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_9  et_pb_toggle_close">
				
				
				
				
				<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">Do You Need A Licence To Undertake My Shop Fit Out Project?</h3>
				<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p><span>ImpeccaBuild is fully insured and licensed, plus when you work with us, you are partnering with a shop fitout company that’s a member of the Master Builders Association (MBA), as well as a member of the Housing Industry Association (HIA). </span></p>
<p><span>What this means for our customers is that we adhere to the highest possible standards at every stage of their shop fitout projects.</span></p>
<p><span>With an excellent understanding of building regulations and legislation, MBA &amp; HIA members also have an excellent knowledge of the broader industry, including innovations and advances which can be used to give you the very best results possible. </span></p>
<p><span>Furthermore, at ImpeccaBuild we only use fully licenced and insured subcontractors for all of our shop fit out projects. </span></p>
<p><span>We strongly advise you not to ever consider using shop fitout companies who aren’t licenced or insured. </span></p>
<p><span>Remember, don’t make the common mistake of choosing an unlicensed contractor because they’re cheaper, only to end up paying more to fix their defective work or their dishonest variation</span></p></div>
			</div>
			</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_3 et_pb_column_45  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_blurb et_pb_blurb_19  et_pb_text_align_left  et_pb_blurb_position_top et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_blurb_content">
					<div class="et_pb_main_blurb_image"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap"><span class="et-waypoint et_pb_animation_off et_pb_animation_off_tablet et_pb_animation_off_phone et-pb-icon">&#x77;</span></span></div>
					<div class="et_pb_blurb_container">
						
						
					</div>
				</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_accordion et_pb_accordion_2">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_10  et_pb_toggle_open">
				
				
				
				
				<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">What’s the difference between a fit out and a renovation?</h3>
				<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p><span>Fit outs and <a href="https://impeccabuild.com.au/office-renovation/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">renovations</a> are two processes that often get confused.</span></p>
<p><span>However, they serve a completely different purpose from each other and require very different procedures.</span></p>
<p><span>The fitout process refers to the internal creation/construction of a space, be it an office, a shop, cafe, or any other commercial space.</span></p>
<p><span>Fitout work can involve flooring, plumbing, painting, electrical, joinery, air-conditioning and more. </span></p>
<p><span>On the other hand, a renovation refers to the refreshing aesthetic aspects of an existing project and is more focused on remodelling rather than building an internal space from scratch.</span></p>
<p><span>A renovation may focus on jobs such as painting walls, selecting materials, furniture and any other processes that are intended to transform the look and feel of a space.</span></p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_11  et_pb_toggle_close">
				
				
				
				
				<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">How Much Will My Shop Fitout Project Cost?</h3>
				<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p><span>No two shop fit outs are ever the same, there are numerous variations that come into play, which makes it difficult to answer questions like how much does a shop fit out cost? </span></p>
<p><span>Costs vary project to project, by size, scope and industry. For example:</span></p>
<ol>
<li><span>a)  A basic office fitout can start at $600 Per Square Metre whereas a premium office fitout could cost you over $2000 Per Square Metre</span></li>
<li><span>b)  A basic retail fitout can start at $1000 Per Square Metre whereas a premium office fitout could cost you over $2000 Per Square Metre</span></li>
<li><span>c) A basic restaurant fitout can start at $1800 Per Square Metre whereas a premium office fitout could cost you over $3400 Per Square Metre</span></li>
</ol>
<p><span>These figures are intended as a guide only. We don’t operate a cookie-cutter approach to our work, providing we treat each client as a unique proposition.</span></p>
<p><span>It’s perfectly possible to mix and match features to create a custom solution that’s exactly right for what you’ve got in mind.</span></p>
<p><span>We provide our clients with a very detailed and accurate costing analysis to clarify any price related queries or concerns prior to commencing their shop fitout project.</span></p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_12  et_pb_toggle_close">
				
				
				
				
				<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">Do I Need Council Approvals For My Shop Fit Out Project ?</h3>
				<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p><span>Typically, you require council approvals for all construction and shop fitout projects where you “change use” of the existing building.</span></p>
<p><span>An example of a “change of use” would be if you change a tenancy which is currently used as an office building into a premises for shop use. </span></p>
<p><span>However, the exact council you require can vary depending on the council, the extent of the works and other factors.</span></p>
<p><span>Top shop fit out companies will organise and liaise with a Private Certifying Authority or council on behalf of their client to simplify the process.</span></p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_13  et_pb_toggle_close">
				
				
				
				
				<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">Should My Shop Fitout Company Be Insured?</h3>
				<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p><span>Don’t be afraid to ask a shop fit out company for copies of their insurance policies.</span></p>
<p><span>Shop fitout companies are required to have public liability insurance, all risk insurance as well as workers compensation.</span></p>
<p><span>If your builder is hesitant to share these documents with you, take this as a major red flag.</span></p>
<p><span>To eliminate any of your concerns, it’s a good idea to cross check with the insurance companies to determine if their policy is still valid or if they’ve expired.</span></p>
<p><span>It’s better to be safe than sorry!</span></p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_14  et_pb_toggle_close">
				
				
				
				
				<h3 class="et_pb_toggle_title">Can We Stay In Our Current Shop During Our Shop Fitout Project?</h3>
				<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p><span>This really depends on the project specifics and scope of work.</span></p>
<p><span>In some cases, it is possible for your business to occupy and continue to trade during your shop fitout. </span></p>
<p><span>We understand that time is money for a business so our team ensures to take extra precautions ensuring your staff are able to work and your business is able to operate as best as possible. </span></p>
<p><span>In cases where we aren’t able to work simultaneously as your business is open, we can arrange for after hours work.</span></p></div>
			</div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div>
				
				
			</div>		</div>
	</div>
